<script>
    $(function(){
        $("#gift_card_nav").click(function(){
            $("body,html").animate({scrollTop: $(".gift_card_tab ").position().top},300);
            $(".headgift_card_tab li:eq(0)").trigger('mouseover').trigger('click');
            $('.tab_content_aagift_card_tab .headcard_tab:eq(0)').find('li:eq(0)').trigger('mouseover').trigger('click');
        });
        $(".gift_card_nav li").click(function(){
            var attr = $(this).attr("data-attr");            
            if(attr != undefined && attr != ""){
               var tabIndexArr = attr.split("-");               
               var $outterTabBar = $(".gift_card_tab .headgift_card_tab").find('li:eq('+tabIndexArr[0]+')');
               if($outterTabBar.html() != ""){
                   $outterTabBar.trigger('mouseover').trigger('click'); //选中一级导航                  
                   if(tabIndexArr[1] != undefined && tabIndexArr[1] != ""){   
                       var secTabObj = $('.tab_content_aagift_card_tab .headcard_tab:eq('+tabIndexArr[0]+')').find('li:eq('+tabIndexArr[1]+')');
                       if(secTabObj.html() != null){
                           secTabObj.trigger('mouseover');
                           secTabObj.trigger('click');
                       }else{
                           return false;
                       }                       
                   }else{
                       var secTabObj = $('.tab_content_aagift_card_tab .headcard_tab:eq('+tabIndexArr[0]+')').find('li:eq(0)');
                       secTabObj.trigger('mouseover');
                       secTabObj.trigger('click');
                   }
               }else{
                   return false;
               }  
              $("body,html").animate({scrollTop: $(".gift_card_tab ").position().top},300);
            }
        });
    });

<script>
    $(function(){
        //点击人气中的礼品卡，页面跳转到相应的所属tab
        $('.linpin_bang .clearfix ul li').click(function(){
            var cardId = $(this).attr("data-id");
            if(cardId){ //如果是具体的某一种卡
                var obj = $('[data-cardid="'+cardId+'"]');
                var cardType = obj.attr("data-cardtype");
                switch(cardType){
                    case "gift_card": //实体卡，两级tab
                        //选中外层tab
                        var cardTabObj = obj.parents(".card_tab");
                        var outerTabClass = cardTabObj.parent().attr("class");                       
                        var index = /tab_(\d+)/.exec(outerTabClass)[1]-1;
                        var tabBarObj = $('.headgift_card_tab li:eq('+index+')');
                        tabBarObj.trigger('mouseover').trigger('click');   
                        
                        //选中内层tab
                        var innerTabContent = obj.parents("[card_type = gift_card]").parent();
                        var innerTabClass = innerTabContent.attr("class");
                        var innerIndex = /tab_(\d+)/.exec(innerTabClass)[1]-1;
                        var innerBar = cardTabObj.find(".headcard_tab ul");
                        if(innerIndex == 0){ //第一个tab
                            var innerTabBarObj = innerBar.find('li:eq(0)');
                        }else if(innerIndex > 0){ //出第一个tab以外的tab
                            var innerTabBarObj = innerBar.find('.tabh_'+innerIndex+'');
                        }
                        innerTabBarObj.trigger('mouseover');
                        innerTabBarObj.trigger('click'); 
                        $("body,html").animate({scrollTop: $(".gift_card_tab ").position().top},200);       
                        break;
                    case "e_card":
                        var cardTabObj = obj.parents("[card_type = e_card]");
                        var outerTabClass = cardTabObj.parent().attr("class");
                        var index = /tab_(\d+)/.exec(outerTabClass)[1]-1;
                        var tabBarObj = $('.heade_card_tab li:eq('+index+')');
                        tabBarObj.trigger('mouseover').trigger('click');
                        $("body,html").animate({scrollTop: $(".e_card_tab ").position().top},300);                        
                        break;
                }
            }
        });  
    });
</script>
